 iske paas se farji aadhaar card, voter card or anya dastavej baraamad hue hai
 The suspect is being questioned in police custody
 sandigdh yuvak mul rup se myanmar kaa rahane vaala he, jo kiraye ke makaan main rah rahaa tha
 SSP Bablu Kumar of Saharanpur said that the suspect's name is Junaid
 vah devband se farji dastavejon ke aadhaar par apana passport banvaanaa chahta tha

 sandigdh ne pichley saal passport ke liye aavedan kiya tha

 iske prapatron kii jaanch main pataa chalaa ki junayd pichley kuch samay se hi darul ulum ke paas sthit ehsaan building main kiraye par rahaa he

 usne farji aadhaar card or anya dastavejon ke aadhaar par passport ke liye aavedan kiya tha

 uske farji dastavej banavaane main kin logon kaa haath rahaa or kin logon ne uski sahaayta kii un par bhi kaarywahi kii jaayegi

 iske baad sakriy aties vahaan par lagaataar chhapemari kar rahi he

 aties team ne chah sandigdh yuvakon ko hiraasat main liya tha

 hiraasat main liye gaye sabhi yuvak madrason ke chaatr bataae gaye the

 iske saath hi ek bangladeshiatankbdula kii giraftaar hui thi
